::

    TYPE LENS :
    STRUCT
        IN     : BOOL; //Inserted state of the Lens
        KNOWN  : BOOL; //Whether state of Lens is definite
        RADIUS : REAL; //Current radius of lens
    END_STRUCT
    END_TYPE

RADII_LIMIT
^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    TYPE RADII_LIMIT :
    STRUCT
        // Trip occurs when the effective radius falls inbetween TRIP_LOW and TRIP_HIGH (inclusive).
        TRIP_LOW  : REAL := 0;     // Trip effective radius low
        TRIP_HIGH : REAL := 10000; // Trip effective radius high
    END_STRUCT
    END_TYPE

    VAR_GLOBAL
        (* Fault handling - inputs *)
        i_xFAULT_CLEAR    			: BOOL;  // Clear fault bit
        i_iUpdateRequestSeq			: DINT;  // Parameter update request sequence number

        (* Fault Handling - active faults *)

        bLimitSummaryFault			: BOOL; // [Active] Whether limit has been violated
        bTableLimitFault 			: BOOL;	// [Active] Energy/lens combination disallowed in table
        bMinEnergyFault 			: BOOL;	// [Active] Minimum energy not met
        bRequiresTransfocatorFault 	: BOOL; // [Active] Transfocator lens required to be inserted

        (* Fault Handling - latched faults *)

        q_bFaultLatch  						: BOOL; // Latch: summary for *any* fault
        q_bStateLatch 						: BOOL;	// Latch: motor state/position unknown
        q_bLimitSummaryFaultLatch    		: BOOL; // Latch: Summary fault due to energy/lens combination
        q_bTableLimitFaultLatch 			: BOOL;	// Latch: Table disallowed range match
        q_bMinEnergyFaultLatch 				: BOOL; // Latch: Minimum energy not met
        q_bRequiresTransfocatorFaultLatch 	: BOOL; // Latch: Transfocator lens required to be inserted

        fbEnergyTables : FB_EnergyTables;

        LENS2_LIMIT : RADII_LIMIT;
        LENS3_LIMIT : RADII_LIMIT;

    END_VAR

POUs

F_EFF_RADIUS
^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    FUNCTION F_EFF_RADIUS : REAL
    VAR_INPUT
        RADII : ARRAY[1..10] OF REAL; // Array of Effective Radii
        COUNT : INT;                 //  Number of Lenses
        IF_NONE: REAL;              //  Radius to report if none inserted (-> infinity)
    END_VAR
    VAR
        INDEX: INT; //Counter for Loop
    END_VAR
    (*F_EFF_RADIUS

    Calculate the effective radius of an array of given lens radii. Non-zero elements
    up to the count value are summed in reciprocal space and then inverted to give the
    final calculation.
    *)

    // Initialize
    F_EFF_RADIUS := 0.0;

    //Sum Reciprocals
    WHILE INDEX < COUNT+1 DO
        //Add non-zero element to total
        IF RADII[INDEX] > 0.0 THEN
            F_EFF_RADIUS := F_EFF_RADIUS + 1/RADII[INDEX];
        END_IF
        //Increment
        INDEX := INDEX + 1;
    END_WHILE

    //Invert if non-zero
    /////////////////////
    IF F_EFF_RADIUS > 0.0 THEN
        F_EFF_RADIUS := 1/F_EFF_RADIUS;
    ELSE
        // B
        F_EFF_RADIUS := IF_NONE;
    END_IF

    END_FUNCTION




F_GetXRTLensIndex
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    FUNCTION F_GetXRTLensIndex : INT
    VAR_INPUT
    END_VAR
    VAR
    END_VAR
    IF XRT_LENS_SYSTEM.LENSES[1].IN THEN
        F_GetXRTLensIndex := 1;
    ELSIF XRT_LENS_SYSTEM.LENSES[2].IN THEN
        F_GetXRTLensIndex := 2;
    ELSIF XRT_LENS_SYSTEM.LENSES[3].IN THEN
        F_GetXRTLensIndex := 3;
    ELSE
        F_GetXRTLensIndex := 0;
    END_IF

    END_FUNCTION

FB_HEARTBEAT
^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_HEARTBEAT
    VAR_INPUT
        BEAT      : BOOL; (*Heartbeat to monitor*)
        DEADTIME  : TIME; (*Acceptable deadtime*)

    END_VAR

    VAR_OUTPUT
        TIME_ON  : TON;
        TIME_OFF : TOF;
        ALIVE    : BOOL;     (*Whether Hearbeat is alive*)
    END_VAR
    (*Hearbeat Monitor

    Monitor a bit which flips back and forth between 0 and 1 .If the deadtime
    passes a certain time limit, report the heartbeat as dead
    *)
    //Timers
    TIME_ON(IN:=BEAT,PT:=DEADTIME);
    TIME_OFF(IN:=BEAT,PT:=DEADTIME);
    //Alive
    ALIVE := NOT TIME_ON.Q AND TIME_OFF.Q;

    END_FUNCTION_BLOCK




FB_LENS_SYSTEM
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_LENS_SYSTEM
    VAR_INPUT
        LENSES : ARRAY[1..10] OF LENS;  //Array of lens structures
        COUNT  : INT;                   //Number of lenses
        IF_NONE : LREAL := 10000.0;	    //Effective radius if no lenses are inserted (instead of infinity)
    END_VAR
    VAR_OUTPUT
        UNKNOWN_FAULT : BOOL;         //Fault for unknown lens state
        EFF_RADII     : REAL; //Calculated effective radii
        IN_COUNT 	  : INT;
    END_VAR
    VAR
        INDEX : INT;                  //Increment for loop
        KNOWN : INT;                  //Number of known lenses
        RADII : ARRAY[1..10] OF REAL; //Inserted Radii
    END_VAR
    (* FB_LENS_SYSTEM

    Monitor an array of lens objects, updating the effective radius and positions of each.
    Both the position of the lenses and the combined radius can cause a fault which is
    communicated to the MPS system.

    *)

    //Check positions of lenses
    ///////////////////////////
    KNOWN := 0; //Tally of known lenses
    IN_COUNT := 0;

    FOR INDEX := 1 TO COUNT BY 1 DO
        IF LENSES[INDEX].IN THEN
            //Inserted lenses are inserted into array
            RADII[INDEX] := LENSES[INDEX].RADIUS;
            IN_COUNT := IN_COUNT + 1;
        ELSE
            //Removed lenses are set to 0.0
            RADII[INDEX] := 0.0;
        END_IF

        // Count all known lenses
        IF LENSES[INDEX].KNOWN THEN
            KNOWN := KNOWN +1;
        END_IF
    END_FOR;

    // Make sure we have accounted for all lenses
    UNKNOWN_FAULT := NOT (COUNT=KNOWN);

    // Calculate effective radii of inserted lens
    //////////////////////////////////////////////
    EFF_RADII := F_EFF_RADIUS(RADII:=RADII, COUNT:=COUNT, IF_NONE:=LREAL_TO_REAL(IF_NONE));

    END_FUNCTION_BLOCK


Related:
    * `F_EFF_RADIUS`_
    * `LENS`_


FB_LimitLookup
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    FUNCTION_BLOCK FB_LimitLookup
    VAR_INPUT
        fEnergy : LREAL;
    END_VAR
    VAR_OUTPUT
        bEnergyInTable : BOOL;
        fLow : LREAL;
        fHigh : LREAL;
    END_VAR
    VAR
        (* TC version doesn't appear to support dynamic arrays here *)
        (* falling back to pointer-handling; sorry! *)
        stRow : POINTER TO ST_TableRow;
        stNextRow : POINTER TO ST_TableRow;
        iRowCount : UINT;
        iRowIdx : UINT;
        fSlope : LREAL;
        fEnergyDelta : LREAL;
        iLensIdx: INT;
    END_VAR
    iLensIdx := F_GetXRTLensIndex();

    IF iLensIdx = 1 THEN
        stRow := ADR(fbEnergyTables.stLENS1_750);
        iRowCount := SIZEOF(fbEnergyTables.stLENS1_750) / SIZEOF(ST_TableRow);
    ELSIF iLensIdx = 2 THEN
        stRow := ADR(fbEnergyTables.stLENS2_428);
        iRowCount := SIZEOF(fbEnergyTables.stLENS2_428) / SIZEOF(ST_TableRow);
    ELSIF iLensIdx = 3 THEN
        stRow := ADR(fbEnergyTables.stLENS3_333);
        iRowCount := SIZEOF(fbEnergyTables.stLENS3_333) / SIZEOF(ST_TableRow);
    ELSE
        stRow := ADR(fbEnergyTables.stNO_LENS);
        iRowCount := SIZEOF(fbEnergyTables.stNO_LENS) / SIZEOF(ST_TableRow);
    END_IF

    fLow := 0.0;
    fHigh := 0.0;
    bEnergyInTable := FALSE;

    IF fEnergy < stRow^.fEnergy THEN
        RETURN;
    END_IF

    FOR iRowIdx := 0 TO iRowCount - 2
    DO
    (*
     result->energy = find_energy;
     double slope = (rows[upper_idx].low - rows[lower_idx].low) / delta_energy;
     result->low = rows[lower_idx].low + slope * (find_energy - rows[lower_idx].energy);

     slope = (rows[upper_idx].high - rows[lower_idx].high) / delta_energy;
     result->high = rows[lower_idx].high + slope * (find_energy - rows[lower_idx].energy);
    *)
        stNextRow := ADR(stRow[1]);
        IF fEnergy >= stRow^.fEnergy AND fEnergy <= stNextRow^.fEnergy THEN
            fEnergyDelta := stNextRow^.fEnergy - stRow^.fEnergy;
            IF fEnergyDelta > 0.0 THEN
                bEnergyInTable := TRUE;
                // Interpolate between the points
                fSlope := (stNextRow^.fLow - stRow^.fLow) / fEnergyDelta;
                fLow := stRow^.fLow + fSlope * (fEnergy - stRow^.fEnergy);

                fSlope := (stNextRow^.fHigh - stRow^.fHigh) / fEnergyDelta;
                fHigh := stRow^.fHigh + fSlope * (fEnergy - stRow^.fEnergy);
            END_IF
            RETURN;
        END_IF
        stRow := stNextRow;
    END_FOR

    END_FUNCTION_BLOCK


Related:
    * `F_GetXRTLensIndex`_
    * `ST_TableRow`_


MAIN
^^^^

::

    PROGRAM MAIN
    VAR
    END_VAR
    (* 16-bit cycle counter *)
    iCycleCount := iCycleCount + 1;

    fbEnergyTables();

    (*  EPICS Rx UPDATE
        Modbus receive
    *)
    p_ModbusRx_OutputCoils();
    p_ModbusRx_PLCMemory();
    p_XLegacyPLCModbus();

    (* Hard-code Lens Radii (microns) *)
    XRT_LENSES[1].RADIUS := 750.0;
    XRT_LENSES[2].RADIUS := 428.6;
    XRT_LENSES[3].RADIUS := 333.3;

    TFS_LENSES[1].RADIUS  := 0.0;   // A pinhole, not a lens.
    TFS_LENSES[2].RADIUS  := 500.0;
    TFS_LENSES[3].RADIUS  := 300.0;
    TFS_LENSES[4].RADIUS  := 250.0;
    TFS_LENSES[5].RADIUS  := 200.0;
    TFS_LENSES[6].RADIUS  := 125.0;
    TFS_LENSES[7].RADIUS  := 62.5;
    TFS_LENSES[8].RADIUS  := 50.0;
    TFS_LENSES[9].RADIUS  := 50.0;
    TFS_LENSES[10].RADIUS := 50.0;

    (* Additional trip settings

        Pre-focus 	Minimum energy [keV] 	Requires transfocator lens low [keV] 	Requires transfocator lens high [keV]
        NO_LENS 	0 	n/a 	n/a
        LENS3_333 	9.5 	9.5 	11.11
        LENS2_428 	8.28 	8.28 	10.02
        LENS1_750 	5.96 	5.96 	8.02

    *)

    (* No XRT lens / no restriction*)
    afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[0].fLow := 0.0;
    afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[0].fHigh := 0.0;
    fMinEnergies[0] := 0.0;

    (* 333.33um Lens 3: 9.5~11.11keV *)
    afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[3].fLow := 9500.0;
    afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[3].fHigh := 11110.0;
    fMinEnergies[3] := 9500.0;

    (* 428um Lens 2: 8.28 ~ 10.02 keV *)
    afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[2].fLow := 8280.0;
    afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[2].fHigh := 10020.0;
    fMinEnergies[2] := 8280.0;

    (* 750um Lens 1: 5.96 ~ 8.02 keV *)
    afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[1].fLow := 5960.0;
    afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[1].fHigh := 8020.0;
    fMinEnergies[1] := 5960.0;


    (*  MPS LOGIC SUMMARY *)
    p_MPSSup();

    (* 	EPICS Tx UPDATE
        Modbus Map Report
        IMPORTANT: This is the LAST subroutine to be called.
    *)
    p_ModbusTx_InputCoils();
    p_ModbusTx_InputReg();
    p_ModbusTx_PLCMemory();

    END_PROGRAM

p_ModbusRx_PLCMemory
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    PROGRAM p_ModbusRx_PLCMemory
    VAR
    END_VAR
    (*
    {"MFX:LENS:",  "XRT_ONLY:LOW" , "aoFLOAT_PORT",    "0", "FLOAT32_LE",  "1", "1000",  "0", "um"}
    {"MFX:LENS:",  "XRT_ONLY:HIGH", "aoFLOAT_PORT",    "2", "FLOAT32_LE",  "1", "1000",  "0", "um"}
    {"MFX:LENS:", "LENS1_750:LOW" , "aoFLOAT_PORT",    "4", "FLOAT32_LE",  "1", "1000",  "0", "um"}
    {"MFX:LENS:", "LENS1_750:HIGH", "aoFLOAT_PORT",    "6", "FLOAT32_LE",  "1", "1000",  "0", "um"}
    {"MFX:LENS:", "LENS2_428:LOW" , "aoFLOAT_PORT",    "8", "FLOAT32_LE",  "1", "1000",  "0", "um"}
    {"MFX:LENS:", "LENS2_428:HIGH", "aoFLOAT_PORT",   "10", "FLOAT32_LE",  "1", "1000",  "0", "um"}
    {"MFX:LENS:", "LENS3_333:LOW" , "aoFLOAT_PORT",   "12", "FLOAT32_LE",  "1", "1000",  "0", "um"}
    {"MFX:LENS:", "LENS3_333:HIGH", "aoFLOAT_PORT",   "14", "FLOAT32_LE",  "1", "1000",  "0", "um"}
    *)
    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[ 0]), destAddr:=ADR(NO_LENS_LIMIT.TRIP_LOW), n:=SIZEOF(NO_LENS_LIMIT.TRIP_LOW));
    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[ 2]), destAddr:=ADR(NO_LENS_LIMIT.TRIP_HIGH), n:=SIZEOF(NO_LENS_LIMIT.TRIP_HIGH));

    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[ 4]), destAddr:=ADR(LENS1_LIMIT.TRIP_LOW), n:=SIZEOF(LENS1_LIMIT.TRIP_LOW));
    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[ 6]), destAddr:=ADR(LENS1_LIMIT.TRIP_HIGH), n:=SIZEOF(LENS1_LIMIT.TRIP_HIGH));

    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[ 8]), destAddr:=ADR(LENS2_LIMIT.TRIP_LOW), n:=SIZEOF(LENS2_LIMIT.TRIP_LOW));
    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[10]), destAddr:=ADR(LENS2_LIMIT.TRIP_HIGH), n:=SIZEOF(LENS2_LIMIT.TRIP_HIGH));

    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[12]), destAddr:=ADR(LENS3_LIMIT.TRIP_LOW), n:=SIZEOF(LENS3_LIMIT.TRIP_LOW));
    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[14]), destAddr:=ADR(LENS3_LIMIT.TRIP_HIGH), n:=SIZEOF(LENS3_LIMIT.TRIP_HIGH));

    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[16]), destAddr:=ADR(i_fPhotonEnergy), n:=SIZEOF(i_fPhotonEnergy));

    MEMCPY(srcAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[18]), destAddr:=ADR(i_iUpdateRequestSeq), n:=SIZEOF(i_iUpdateRequestSeq));

    END_PROGRAM

p_ModbusTx_InputCoils

    PROGRAM p_ModbusTx_InputCoils
    VAR
    END_VAR
    VAR_OUTPUT
    END_VAR
    (** NOTE: These values are mirrored in PLC memory output as well. **)
    (** From an EPICS client perspective, it's easier to keep the data
        in synchronization when sent in one packet. The IOC now uses
        those values and these are vestigial for now.
    **)

p_ModbusTx_PLCMemory
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    PROGRAM p_ModbusTx_PLCMemory
    VAR
    END_VAR
    (* Send status information over modbus to IOC *)

    (* The calculated effective radius *)
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[100]), srcAddr:=ADR(XRT_RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(XRT_RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[102]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_RADIUS));

    (* Individual lens radius *)
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[104]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[1].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[1].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[106]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[2].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[2].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[108]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[3].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[3].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[110]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[4].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[4].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[112]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[5].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[5].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[114]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[6].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[6].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[116]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[7].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[7].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[118]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[8].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[8].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[120]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[9].RADIUS),  n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[9].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[122]), srcAddr:=ADR(TFS_LENSES[10].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(TFS_LENSES[10].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[124]), srcAddr:=ADR(XRT_LENSES[1].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(XRT_LENSES[1].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[126]), srcAddr:=ADR(XRT_LENSES[2].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(XRT_LENSES[2].RADIUS));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[128]), srcAddr:=ADR(XRT_LENSES[3].RADIUS), n:=SIZEOF(XRT_LENSES[3].RADIUS));

    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[130]), srcAddr:=ADR(q_stActiveLimit.TRIP_LOW), n:=SIZEOF(q_stActiveLimit.TRIP_LOW));
    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[132]), srcAddr:=ADR(q_stActiveLimit.TRIP_HIGH), n:=SIZEOF(q_stActiveLimit.TRIP_HIGH));

    // MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[134]), srcAddr:=ADR(iCycleCount), n:=SIZEOF(iCycleCount));
    // Abuse the FLOAT port to send along 16-bit cycle information:
    mb_PLC_Memory[134] := iCycleCount;
    mb_PLC_Memory[135] := 0;

    MEMCPY(destAddr:=ADR(mb_PLC_Memory[136]), srcAddr:=ADR(i_fPhotonEnergy), n:=SIZEOF(i_fPhotonEnergy));
    // 137 taken up by fPhotonEnergy

    (* Online/active values *)
    mb_PLC_Memory[138]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(bHeartbeatAlive);
    mb_PLC_Memory[139]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(bFAULT);
    mb_PLC_Memory[140]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(bStateFault);
    mb_PLC_Memory[141]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(bLimitSummaryFault);
    mb_PLC_Memory[142]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(bMinEnergyFault);
    mb_PLC_Memory[143]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(bRequiresTransfocatorFault);
    mb_PLC_Memory[144]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(bTableLimitFault);
    mb_PLC_Memory[145]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(FALSE);
    mb_PLC_Memory[146]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(FALSE);
    mb_PLC_Memory[147]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(FALSE);

    (* Latched fault information *)
    mb_PLC_Memory[148]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(q_bHeartbeatLatch);
    mb_PLC_Memory[149]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(q_bFaultLatch);
    mb_PLC_Memory[150]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(q_bStateLatch);
    mb_PLC_Memory[151]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(q_bLimitSummaryFaultLatch);
    mb_PLC_Memory[152]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(q_bMinEnergyFaultLatch);
    mb_PLC_Memory[153]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(q_bRequiresTransfocatorFaultLatch);
    mb_PLC_Memory[154]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(q_bTableLimitFaultLatch);
    mb_PLC_Memory[155]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(FALSE);
    mb_PLC_Memory[156]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(FALSE);
    mb_PLC_Memory[157]:=BOOL_TO_WORD(FALSE);

    END_PROGRAM




p_MPSSup
^^^^^^^^

::

    PROGRAM p_MPSSup
    VAR
        BEAT: FB_HEARTBEAT;
        fbHeartbeatLatch : RS;
        fbFaultLatch : RS;
        fbStateLatch : RS;
        fbLimitLatch : RS;
        fbTableLimitFaultLatch : RS;
        fbMinEnergyFaultLatch : RS;
        fbRequiresTransfocatorFaultLatch : RS;
        rtUpdate : R_TRIG;
        iLastSeq : DINT;
        bUpdateRequest: BOOL;

        LIMIT_FAULT : BOOL;

        fEnergyMin : LREAL;
        fRequiresTransfocatorEnergyLow : LREAL;
        fRequiresTransfocatorEnergyHigh : LREAL;
        fTripLow : LREAL;
        fTripHigh : LREAL;
        bEnergyInTable : BOOL;

        iLensIdx: INT;
        fbLimitLookup : FB_LimitLookup;

    END_VAR
    // Latch fault state
    ////////////////////

    fbFaultLatch(SET:=bFAULT, RESET1:=i_xFAULT_CLEAR);
    q_bFaultLatch := fbFaultLatch.Q1;

    fbHeartbeatLatch(SET:=NOT bHeartbeatAlive, RESET1:=i_xFAULT_CLEAR);
    q_bHeartbeatLatch := fbHeartbeatLatch.Q1;

    fbStateLatch(SET:=bStateFault, RESET1:=i_xFAULT_CLEAR);
    q_bStateLatch := fbStateLatch.Q1;

    fbLimitLatch(SET:=bLimitSummaryFault, RESET1:=i_xFAULT_CLEAR);
    q_bLimitSummaryFaultLatch := fbLimitLatch.Q1;

    fbTableLimitFaultLatch(SET:=bTableLimitFault, RESET1:=i_xFAULT_CLEAR);
    q_bTableLimitFaultLatch := fbTableLimitFaultLatch.Q1;

    fbMinEnergyFaultLatch(SET:=bMinEnergyFault, RESET1:=i_xFAULT_CLEAR);
    q_bMinEnergyFaultLatch := fbMinEnergyFaultLatch.Q1;

    fbRequiresTransfocatorFaultLatch(SET:=bRequiresTransfocatorFault, RESET1:=i_xFAULT_CLEAR);
    q_bRequiresTransfocatorFaultLatch := fbRequiresTransfocatorFaultLatch.Q1;

    //IOC Heartbeat:
    BEAT(BEAT:=i_xIOC_HEARTBEAT, DEADTIME:=TIME#1.0S);
    bHeartbeatAlive := BEAT.ALIVE;

    //XRT LENS SYSTEM
    ///////////////////////////
    XRT_LENS_SYSTEM(LENSES:=XRT_LENSES, COUNT:=3);
    XRT_RADIUS := XRT_LENS_SYSTEM.EFF_RADII; (* Propagated to EPICS *)

    //TFS LENS SYSTEM
    ///////////////////////////
    TFS_LENS_SYSTEM(LENSES:=TFS_LENSES, COUNT:=10, IF_NONE:=10000.0);
    TFS_RADIUS := TFS_LENS_SYSTEM.EFF_RADII; (* Propagated to EPICS *)

    (* Reset our tracking variables *)
    bTableLimitFault := FALSE;
    bMinEnergyFault := FALSE;
    bRequiresTransfocatorFault := FALSE;

    (* Determine which XRT lens is inserted, and pick the correct range based on it. *)

    IF NOT XRT_LENS_SYSTEM.UNKNOWN_FAULT THEN
        iLensIdx := F_GetXRTLensIndex();
        fbLimitLookup(
            fEnergy:=i_fPhotonEnergy,
            fLow=>fTripLow,
            fHigh=>fTripHigh,
            bEnergyInTable=>bEnergyInTable
        );

        q_stActiveLimit.TRIP_LOW := LREAL_TO_REAL(fTripLow);
        q_stActiveLimit.TRIP_HIGH := LREAL_TO_REAL(fTripHigh);

        IF bEnergyInTable AND fTripHigh > fTripLow THEN
            // Lens inserted and trip region specified:
            bTableLimitFault := (fTripLow <= TFS_RADIUS AND TFS_RADIUS <= fTripHigh);
        END_IF

        fEnergyMin := fMinEnergies[iLensIdx];
        fRequiresTransfocatorEnergyLow := afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[iLensIdx].fLow;
        fRequiresTransfocatorEnergyHigh := afbRequiresLensEnergyRange[iLensIdx].fHigh;

        (*
        Regardless of transfocator setting, the minimum energy must be
        greater than or equal to that shown in the table (Minimum energy [keV]).
        Trip if below.
        *)
        bMinEnergyFault := i_fPhotonEnergy < fEnergyMin;

        (*
        When a pre-focusing lens is inserted, there exists a range of photon
        energies in which at least one transfocator lens must be inserted.
        If the current photon energy is within this (inclusive) range and no
        lens is inserted, trip.
        *)
        IF fRequiresTransfocatorEnergyHigh > fRequiresTransfocatorEnergyLow THEN
            (* Check that we're in the given photon energy range *)
            IF fRequiresTransfocatorEnergyLow <= i_fPhotonEnergy AND i_fPhotonEnergy <= fRequiresTransfocatorEnergyHigh THEN
                (* And if so, trip when IN_COUNT == 0 *)
                bRequiresTransfocatorFault := (TFS_LENS_SYSTEM.IN_COUNT < 1);
            END_IF
        END_IF

    END_IF

    //Summarize faults
    ///////////////////////////

    bLimitSummaryFault := (
        bTableLimitFault OR         // Inside the table-defined trip range
        bMinEnergyFault OR          // Below minimum required energy for XRT lens
        bRequiresTransfocatorFault  // Require transfocator lens in this range
    );

    //State Violations
    bStateFault := (
        XRT_LENS_SYSTEM.UNKNOWN_FAULT OR  // XRT lens state unknown
        TFS_LENS_SYSTEM.UNKNOWN_FAULT OR  // Transfocator lens state unknown
        XRT_LENS_SYSTEM.IN_COUNT > 1      // Unexpected lens count
    );

    //Final Summary

    // MPS trips when *LOW*.
    //  So: bTRIP_MPS (False) when bFAULT (True)
    //  And bTRIP_MPS (True) when bFAULT (False)
    bFAULT := bLimitSummaryFault OR bStateFault OR NOT bHeartbeatAlive;
    bTRIP_MPS := NOT bFAULT;

    END_PROGRAM


Related:
    * `FB_HEARTBEAT`_
    * `FB_LimitLookup`_
    * `F_GetXRTLensIndex`_
    * `LENS`_


p_XLegacyPLCModbus
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

::

    PROGRAM p_XLegacyPLCModbus
    VAR
        fbLegacyPLCInputCoilsRx	:	FB_MBReadCoils;

        i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits	:	ARRAY [0..20] OF BYTE;

        ftReset	: F_TRIG;

    END_VAR
    (* Modbus Info for Koyo
    Modbus Addresses for
    Koyo DL05/06/240/250/260/430/440/450 PLCs
    PLC Memory Type		| Modbus start address Decimal (octal) | Function codes
    Inputs (X)			  2048 (04000)							2
    Special Relays (SP)	  3072 (06000)							2
    Outputs (Y)			  2048 (04000)							1, 5, 15
    Control Relays (C)	  3072 (06000)							1, 5, 15
    Timer Contacts (T)	  6144 (014000)							1, 5, 15
    Counter Contacts (CT) 6400 (014400)							1, 5, 15
    Stage Status Bits (S) 6144 (012000)							1, 5, 15
    *)

    ftReset(CLK:=fbLegacyPLCInputCoilsRx.bBusy);

    fbLegacyPLCInputCoilsRx.bExecute := TRUE;

    fbLegacyPLCInputCoilsRx(sIPAddr:='172.21.62.99', nTCPPort:=502, nQuantity:=32, nMBAddr:=8#6000, cbLength:=SIZEOF(i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits),  pDestAddr:=ADR(i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits), tTimeout:=T#10S);

    IF fbLegacyPLCInputCoilsRx.bError THEN
        //run some error code for modbus
        //if there's a modbus error, set all incoming bits to zero, set
        // HXX PLC Relay coil C[10] is used for MXT:GCC:06.VacOK
        i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits[0].0 := 0;
        i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits[0].1 := 0;
        i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits[0].2 := 0;
        i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits[0].3 := 0;
        i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits[0].4 := 0;
        i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits[1].0 := 0;
        i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits[1].1 := 0;
        i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits[1].2 := 0;



    ELSIF ftReset.Q AND fbLegacyPLCInputCoilsRx.cbRead > 0 THEN
        fbLegacyPLCInputCoilsRx.bExecute := FALSE;

        //i_xUSVacOK := i_xLegacyPLC_CnBits[1].0;

    ELSE
        //more error code cause we didn't manage to read anything
    END_IF

    END_PROGRAM
